                static wrap(orig: $tsmb_folder) {
                        const copy = new $tsmb_folder_draft
                        copy.orig = () => orig
                        copy.id = () => orig.id()

                        return new $tsmb_folder

                        if (next !== undefined) return next

                }

                commit() {
                        this.orig()?.dto(this.dto())

$memento_notes $mol_book2_catalog
  auto /
    <= content_flush null




    @$mol_mem
    current_id( id?: string ): string {
      return id || ''
    }

    @$mol_mem_key
    content( id: any, next?: any ) {
      this.current_id( id )
      const memento_data = this.getMementoData( this.current_id( id ) )
      const path = this.$.$memento_config_baseMementosDir + '/' + id
      const data = this.$.$mol_state_local.value( id, next ) ?? $memento_lib_tauri.base().readTextFile(
        path + '/' + memento_data.md_content_path,
        { dir: $memento_lib_tauri.base().BaseDirectory.App }
      )
      return data
    }

    @$mol_mem
    content_flush() {
      this.$.$mol_wait_timeout( 1000 )
      const id = this.current_id()
      const memento_data = this.getMementoData( id )
      const path = this.$.$memento_config_baseMementosDir + '/' + id
      this.log("flush data ", this.content( id ))
      $memento_lib_tauri.fs().writeTextFile( path + '/' + memento_data.md_content_path, this.content( id ), { dir: $memento_lib_tauri.base().BaseDirectory.App } )
    }
